Fair to say that a lot of hotels in China have the hardware (nice rooms and good facilities etc) but normally get let down by the software (service). This was an exception. Had serious issues with health codes and covid testing in Wuxi but Shumaila (Guest Service Manager) along with her Chinese colleague turned into Superwoman and Superman and went way beyond the levels of expected service for a 5 star hotel. First they accompanied me to the covid testing point (1 km away) but didnt stop there because i still had problems and had to go to the hospital to get tested (4 kms away). They helped order a taxi and Shumaila actually went to the hospital with me to ensure everything was ok! Also this was all done on her day off! Remarkable. 

Throughout my stay the service in the hotel was excellent whether it be at check in or out (quick) or in the restaurant and/or executive lounge area. Everyone in the hotel had a smile on their face and was willing to be of assistance. 

Food including breakfast had variety and was good

Keep up the excellent work, well done to Shumaila and your hotel team

posted:Posted June 4, 2024
msg:I stayed at the Radisson Collection Hotel Wuxi on Junting Middle Road not long ago. The feeling is really hard to describe. When planning the hotel, I only considered the InterContinental Hotel Wuxi Junlai because it is just in the city center and near Nanchan Temple. The facilities of other brand hotels are too old, so I decisively considered this brand hotel that was established in 2021. It is not a five-star hotel. I went to the front desk to check in on the day of check-in. I only felt the indifference and expressionlessness of the staff. After checking in, I didn’t tell me where the elevator was. During the period, there were many staff walking around in the hotel lobby and ignoring us. I want to emphasize that I was the only one who checked in at that time. Then all the things happened after we returned to the hotel at night. 

1⃣️ My mother went to the bathroom to take a shower and forgot to put the anti-slip mat at the door of the bathroom. At that time, she was barefoot at the door of the bathroom. So, in order to prevent slipping, I squatted on the tiles to wipe the water stains. What caught my eye was that the white towel in my hand became dirtier and dirtier. My God, how long has it been since no one stayed in this room? Even the basic room cleaning was not done. I told the manager on duty that day everything that happened. It was a man. He wanted to change our room without saying a word. The result was a bit funny. We waited for more than 20 minutes for the concierge's cart when we changed rooms and everything was packed. During this period, I contacted the switchboard many times and the reply was "Ah, the front desk didn't contact you. Sorry, I'll ask for you again." The concierge cart took only two minutes to go upstairs, but we waited for more than 20 minutes. Finally, the staff came upstairs embarrassedly. During this period, the switchboard and the front desk never asked a question. It seemed that no one cared about the guest's complaint. No one approached or handled it.

2⃣️ During the three days and two nights of staying in the hotel, only my parents went to have breakfast. The restaurant staff who received them for two consecutive days were female staff with a bad attitude and even ignored them. If the guests went to have breakfast early in the morning and faced a world-weary face, would they feel good? There were very few people having breakfast, but this staff member was not polite at all and didn't even know his job responsibilities. After I left, I directly complained to the restaurant manager about this matter. I don't know if they will improve later, but I complained.

3⃣️I would like to ask which hotel's switchboard goes off work before 8 o'clock in the evening, and the switchboard work becomes the work of the front desk staff The funniest thing is that no one answered the phone when I called. After six times, I finally got the phone but was told that they were busy. I just asked the room service to send me six bottles of water. It took half an hour to send them. If there is no one on duty at the switchboard and the front desk is responsible for management, it is caused by the chaotic internal management of your hotel. There is no connection between the departments. It is so chaotic that I have to ask again and again for a few bottles of water. If the night bed service is done well, I don’t need to ask for water when I return to the hotel at night. Basic night bed service at least requires replacements and drinking water by the bedside, but you don’t have any of them, and you don’t even know or understand them. Don’t you feel guilty for charging this price? The funniest thing is that there is no so-called executive lounge privilege because it is not open at all. I only knew all this after I booked the room.

4⃣️I have to complain to the front office department. Your front office department is really not as good as the cleaning lady of the room service. The cleaning lady will greet politely, but all the staff of the front office department, including the duty manager, pretend not to see it. There are not many guests in the hotel. How can you make guests feel good? Basic courtesy has no value.

The above is a summary of the problems I encountered during my three-day and two-night stay. I hope the hotel's related departments will know and pay attention to it. The low occupancy rate has a lot to do with your poor service. If it's not a five-star hotel, why would the room card have to be related to Radisson? I really can't understand why the hotel's external signs also have the Radisson logo. On the last day, I met with the hotel restaurant manager at noon. What's funny is that the director of housekeeping and the front office manager both showed up. Before that, no one negotiated with me or even took the initiative to understand the situation. Indeed, seeing that I'm leaving, it's not wrong to do some superficial work, but guests are not stupid. Such a hotel will not have repeat customers.

msg:During this trip to Wuxi, I was fortunate enough to stay at the Radisson Collection Hotel and experience an unforgettable and wonderful time. From booking to check-out, the whole process was extremely smooth and made me look forward to this trip.

**Excellent location**
The hotel is located in the heart of Wuxi City with convenient transportation. It is extremely convenient to travel to Wuxi's famous attractions such as Lingshan Buddha and Three Kingdoms City, or to explore local food and shopping venues. There are bus stops and subway stations near the hotel, allowing me to easily visit every corner of Wuxi.

**Rooms are comfortable and spacious**
The rooms you stay in are spacious and bright, and the decoration style is modern yet warm. The bedding is soft and comfortable, ensuring that I can have a good sleep every night. The facilities in the room are well-equipped, whether it is high-speed Wi-Fi, large-screen TV or minibar, they all made me feel the convenience and comfort of home.

**Warm and thoughtful service**
The service attitude of the hotel staff is excellent. From the front desk reception to the room service, every employee shows professionalism and enthusiasm. Not only did they provide detailed travel information, they also took the initiative to help me solve some minor problems, which made me feel attentive and caring.

**Delicious and diverse meals**
The restaurant in the hotel provides a variety of dining options, whether it is a buffet for breakfast or exquisite Chinese food for dinner, I was fully satisfied. The ingredients are fresh and the dishes are delicious, especially the local Wuxi cuisine, which gave me a deeper understanding of Wuxi’s food culture.

**full facilities**
The hotel's fitness center and swimming pool are well maintained, allowing me to maintain my daily exercise routine while traveling.

Summarize:
Radisson Collection Hotel Wuxi is undoubtedly a highlight of my trip to Wuxi. Whether it is hardware facilities or software services, I am very satisfied. If I have the opportunity to come to Wuxi again, I will definitely choose this place as my stay again. Highly recommended to everyone planning to travel to Wuxi!

msg:It was only a one-night stay, so I decided to go with it. I have stayed at other hotels in Wuxi in the past and found the facilities and services to be average. This time I chose Radisson Blu because it is relatively new, and it did not disappoint!
Probably because during the Chinese New Year period, there were only two check-in counters. After a short wait, it was my turn, and the staff decisively upgraded my reservation to a suite. It was also a very happy New Year gift!
The room is very spacious, but the decoration style is more business-like and a bit old-fashioned, which is not my cup of tea.
The hardware is complete and very new. The room has a good view, overlooking the entire Xishan District. It is especially beautiful at sunrise in the early morning. I don't know if it's because of the suite, but the sound insulation is very good and I slept comfortably all night.
The breakfast room is very large and can accommodate many guests. It was almost full at seven o'clock. The food selection is relatively standard, with both Chinese and Western options. The meat filling of the small wontons can almost exceed the size of the normal large wontons, and there are also old noodles Wuxi large meat buns (but out of curiosity, there are no xiaolongbao￼), and they all taste pretty good~
This is a very cost-effective one-time trip to Radisson Blu!

msg:衹能説一般般
房間很大，電視很小
酒店很豪，服務一般
餐飲很貴，感受一般

在這裏的感受用一句話來總結：標配標配衹有標配，若有需要，拿錢來換；想要笑臉，絕對很難。

老闆衹想要掙錢，員工衹想要偷懶，客人最好默默進來默默出去，交錢辦事，不給任何人添麻煩。

這裏放在最顯眼的地方的都是收費項目，茶几上的不是果盤是spA項目介紹，冰箱裏的不是飲料，是客房送餐的服務項目。

員工臉上看到的不是笑臉，是你幹嘛又來給我添麻煩！

所以我收拾收拾默默離開，不是你們不適合我，是我不適合你們，你們需要有錢而又麻木滴客仁，而我恰好不是⊙ω⊙

45平米的主題親子房（含衣帽間），如果2大2小入住，是比較侷促的，外加有不少主題裝飾物，看起來就更緊湊了。
衣帽間深得我愛，尤其冬天入住，衣帽間太好用了～
離開酒店的後一晚，發現自己的身體乳掉在酒店了，因為是新開封，於是電話酒店詢問是否還有保留，1/23入住，1/25致電酒店，到目前為止，酒店還沒有給到任何回覆，這一來，反倒是讓我對接線員詢問的“你着急嗎”這話產生了些許奇思妙想。

msg:總體感覺三星級亞朵酒店標準，硬湊成五星級酒店！無錫是沒有能打的酒店了嗎？
圖一：早餐餐費100元，水果不新鮮，是冰凍的。早上對管理人員説了，她説要的話給我打包一份，我缺的不是水果，而是新鮮水果。以至於吃下後就找衞生間，一樓的衞生間沒有清理乾淨。打開一個門，是沒沖凈的。裏面還有煙頭。
圖二：馬桶太小，旁邊的控制器看不清楚。非要拍個照片看。
圖三：水吧的咖啡機第一個膠囊下去，打出來的是水而且夾雜着雜質。
圖四：水吧上的燈開關依舊沒找到！！！打了電話問客服，客服也不知道在哪兒。
第五：是地下負二層的停車位太少，打過電話問過了，衹有區區一排幾個。還有停負一層，需要到一樓，再跑過大廳，再去按電梯上樓，這樣很不合理。
第六：是打電話需要浴鹽的時候，十分鐘送到。以至於浴缸的水都滿了才送來。

name:G‍u‍e‍s‍t‍ ‍U‍s‍e‍r
info:Collection Superior Room
info:Stayed in May 2023
info:Solo travelers
info:2 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted May 27, 2023
msg:最近住過的最滿意的酒店了
硬件方面：2021年開業的新酒店，設施配置整體更加先進，印象深的是房間的層高，最少3.1米，很舒服，要了邊套城景，也沒有突兀的大柱子，建築結構非常優秀。哈曼卡頓的音響帶無線充電，很人性化。衣帽間兩個雙門廚，足夠放行李。房間四十多平也很寬敞。衞浴是樂家，衹能説相對一般，智能馬桶還可以。戴森的電吹風很nice 整體細節還是很用心的，床墊感覺適中，不是很軟。一邊三個枕頭，總記六個，彰顯豪氣。唯一美中不足的是咖啡機的膠囊有點拉垮。
深夜入住，免費升房，送一份早餐，人性的服務非常好。整體色調也很暖色，實木木皮紋理，牀頭櫃用了雀眼染色木皮高光，一下提高了傢俱檔次。
總之很棒的居住體驗，雖然衹有幾個小時還是印象非常好

1、入住時，前台並沒有主動告知從哪邊上電梯去房間，連早餐在哪，幾點開始結束也不説，還是我自己問的。
2、訂的親子房，進房間後感覺是拿其他房間湊的親子房，衹放了一個帳篷，一個積木桌，裏面並沒有小朋友的東西，小朋友拖鞋也沒有，電話前台，回覆是還在採購中，有親子房這些基本的東西不是應該常備的嗎，所以特意查了下之前別人2月份的評價，回覆也是採購中，那請問你們一個小童用品要採購幾個月嗎？衞生間也沒有像圖片裏那樣的親子用品，倒是放了一套小朋友們洗漱，沒有漱口杯子，請問我是要怎麼用呢？房間的床頭邊放了一個小木箱，還鎖起來了，有個牌子是尋寶，但是打開啥也沒有，請問這是裝飾嗎？意義何在？
3、另外住的那天晚上還點了個外賣，顯示放在酒店專門放外賣的前台，本來説自己下去拿，但是電話前台説是有機器人送上去了，結果等了半天也不見送上來，再次電話前台，説是機器人餐多，還在一層層送，我都等了半小時，還是沒有，第三次電話，跟我説搞錯了，還沒送，還在下面前台，馬上由工作人員送，結果工作人員還把別人的外賣送到我們房間，幸虧我沒拆啊，我要是拆了你們酒店跟其他客人怎麼説呢，我衹能又電話前台告訴他們送錯了，把送錯的放門外讓他們拿走。
下次不會再住這個酒店了，當然人家也不缺我這一個客人。

msg:衞生：需要提高，淋浴間有點異味，水槽有頭髮。


服務：滿意，迎賓、前台都可以。入住期間剛好生日，自己沒有意識到，早餐的服務員提醒了我還專門準備了生日麪。


設施：電動窗紗壞了，問題不大。哈曼卡頓的藍牙音箱很方便，聽歌遊戲都挺好。電視頻道可以，沒高清。枕頭種類不少，但幾個枕頭的高矮軟硬都差不多，個人覺得普遍偏硬。床墊個人覺得偏硬，布料有點涼，這個在冬季還是挺重要的，希望能區分一下，冬季更換不同布料的四件套。

早餐:贊👍，無論種類、口味、服務都能滿足多數人需求，西餐不粗糙，冷盤麪包沙拉水果醬料都提供多種選擇。更推薦中餐，蒸煮煎炸炒幾乎都有，糕點，麪條，煎餃，油條，春捲，四五種炒菜，粥，酒糟湯圓等等吧，很不錯。

name:M‍e‍n‍g‍t‍o‍n‍g
info:Collection Elite Room
info:Stayed in November 2022
info:Business travelers
info:2 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted November 24, 2022
msg:21-23日出差無錫。攜程上重點關注了 麗笙和凱悦。凱悦住過，麗笙酒店比較新（去年才開業）。電話諮詢了麗笙，得到麗笙前台 小孫熱情詳細地介紹並告知無錫防疫政策。然後下單麗笙精選行政精英房。入住當天在前台碰到 小孫，告知已經按照要求事先安排好了房間，28樓最高樓層，且主動提供離酒店最近的核酸檢測點，包括開放時間，這個要給大大的贊。酒店硬件很好，自動馬桶，自動窗簾，膠囊咖啡機，房間配有空氣凈化器。早餐豐富，該有都有，臨走前可以咖啡打包。但竟然沒有無錫本地特色的小籠？服務員很客氣，無論電梯還是走廊，都主打招呼問好，客房服務不錯，有夜床服務。需要吐槽的是行政酒廊待遇，因為疫情原因，27樓酒廊未開放。作為備案，下午茶放一樓大堂，但下午茶實在寒酸，2杯咖啡（可選）+1小碟餅乾（5-6片）。去問了服務員怎麼這麼少？完全不符合酒廊配備，酒廊裏至少2個點心+2個乾果，水果+軟飲的配置。服務員説軟飲可以+，但確實衹有這些，後來覺得不好意思，拿了點乾果過來，也難為她了。晚上歡樂時光放在2樓中餐廳，酒店有套餐（開胃菜，熱菜，湯，主食，水果），菜品不錯。但放在中餐廳太正式了，少了歡樂時光的輕鬆的氣氛。酒店整體很好，下次出差還住這裏。
----------------------------------------

name:|‍m‍u‍|‍y‍i‍|
info:Selected Superior Twin Room
info:Stayed in December 2021
info:Couples
info:14 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted January 2, 2022
msg:服務：無錫的豪華酒店裡算很好的，進到大堂就會有人過來引導，早餐的時候也有很全面的服務，希望能一直保持。
硬件：比較新，房間裏這個價位這樣的裝修，還是很不錯，軟裝也很用心，吹風機是戴森的算個亮點吧，不過浴缸有點黑色的痕跡，本來想泡澡，看到了還是算了。
早餐：市區酒店裡麪早餐算不錯的，好幾個明檔，有專門的服務人員現吃現做，種類非常豐富，味道好，食材棒。
順便説下，2樓日料自助還可以。
最後，贈飲的水是不是可以升級成其他品牌的“礦泉水”，不是冰露不好，就是這個價位想喝口礦泉水，這個要求應該不過分吧。。。
----------------------------------------

總體來説，值得來體驗一下。
